### ONE-PAGE DIAGNOSIS ‚Äî why RUN-5 non-converged (the gate WORKED; the roots are structural, terrain-level)
**What went RIGHT (the machine is sound):** fresh_go_5 ran a clean cold bedroom‚Üí8-badges in ~3.1h wall (11,312s, 0 tracebacks, 0 hard wedges ‚Äî the NS#7 self.trav crash + NS#16 leg2 livelock were both fixed/unwedged this night). Final party **[venusaur L65, pidgeotto L33, lapras L26, kadabra L35, fearow L33, dugtrio L34] ‚Äî SIX DISTINCT species, 0 duplicates, dex 15.** The **E4-READINESS GATE performed exactly as designed**: at `head_to_league` it fired RED (floor L26 < target L50, gap 39), **CAPPED the ace flat at L65 (0 XP)**, ran the ace-capped bench grind, and when the reachable grind couldn't converge it **STOOD DOWN LOUD ‚Äî refusing to enter the League under-shape** (line 123312). No under-shape entry, no silent loop, no solo-ace L100. That is a SUCCESS of the qualifying firewall.

**What FAILED (the residual root RUN-5's two fixes could not reach ‚Äî a TERRAIN-ADEQUACY catch-22):**
1. **The floor mon is un-catch-up-able on pre-VR terrain.** Lapras was caught **fresh at L25 in the Safari (~badge 6)** and never had the runway to climb from L25‚ÜíL50 while the ace was already L61+. At the badge-8 gate the fix-(a) reroute correctly walked to the nearest open grass (**Route 2**, edge north) ‚Äî but **Route 2 wilds top ~L13**, so a L26 mon earns ~zero XP. Log shows **19 "made NO progress / un-grindable"** markers; the floor L26 **never moved across all 8 stints**. This is the exact wall RUN-5's own orders foresaw: *"no open grass in Kanto exceeds ~L30; the only high-level grass is the VR CAVE."* Fix (a) can only close a SMALL residual gap ‚Äî here the gap was 24 levels (L26‚ÜíL50), far beyond what any open grass in Kanto can feed.
2. **Fix (b) (order-3b relax, hand the bench XP on the back-half marches) didn't hold the gap** because the badge-6‚Üí8 back-half is mostly **ace-led terrain** ‚Äî the Seafoam sea crossing, the Blaine/Giovanni gym-LEADER fights, and the Giovanni R21 sea reroute all field the ace, and Lapras entered that stretch already ~35 levels behind. The relax fired on open legs but there simply weren't enough open-ground battles to move a fresh L25 catch to L50.

**THE STRUCTURAL FIX (for Jonny's ATTENDED adjudication ‚Äî do NOT ship blind):** the cleanest root fix is **terrain-adequacy in the gate-grind**: when the E4-prep grind is starved (no open grass adequate for the floor's level), let it route the ace-capped bench grind INTO the **Victory Road cave** (step-encounter grind, ~L40+ wilds ‚Äî the only Kanto terrain that can level a L26‚ÜíL50) ‚Äî i.e. the ace-cap must OVERRIDE the map-type "ace-leads-in-caves" rule *specifically inside the gate-grind*, so the bench fights the VR wilds with the ace held. Secondary/complementary: (B) don't seat a fresh late Safari catch (Lapras L25) as a permanent endgame party member without a dedicated adequate-terrain catch-up BEFORE the gate; (C) revisit whether the ace should be allowed to reach L65 on the back-half at all (a tighter ace-cap earlier keeps target=ace‚àí15 lower). Root (1) is the load-bearing one ‚Äî Kanto has no open grass that closes a 24-level floor gap, so the gate-grind MUST reach cave-level terrain or the floor can never qualify.
